**Candidate 97:** T*c0*log(c1*epsilon+1) + c2*epsilon^c3 + c4*epsilon^c5 + c6*log(c1*epsilon+1).

GT = 90.776*epsilon² + 2.482*T*log(epsilon+1) - 838.686*log(epsilon+1).

Match: c0=2.482, c2=90.776, c6=-838.686. Set c4=0 (or c5 to anything with c4=0).

This works! T*c0*log(epsilon+1) + c2*epsilon² + c6*log(epsilon+1) = c0*T*log(epsilon+1) + c6*log(epsilon+1) + c2*epsilon² = (c0*T + c6)*log(epsilon+1) + c2*epsilon² = c0*(T + c6/c0)*log(epsilon+1) + c2*epsilon² = c0*(T - 337.769)*log(epsilon+1) + c2*epsilon².

**YES! This matches!**

Candidate 97 verdict: [MATCH]
